When rain was expected, she texted that she'd left an umbrella outside my door. She did a little research and suggested places I would enjoy in the area. We had 4 people (2 couples) and it although it's a small space we didn't feel claustrophobic and there were enough personal touches to make you thankful to not be in a hotel room. Although there are 3 places to lay your head, only one bed is really comfortable for sleeping so it is probably ideal for 1 or 2 people. The location is perfect - coffee shop, juice shop, and a great bar right downstairs and a few blocks from lovely beach access and anything you may want to do in Long Beach! The parking situation is not the best, but as a non-Californian I'm thinking that is just the way things are out there.</p><span data-reactid="1881">Mel</span><span data-reactid="1882">2014-08-28T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1883"><p data-reactid="1884">Great place could use a microwave, a tv, a a new window replaced. It's in the middle of everything witch was convinient, but very noisy even with the windows closed. Other than that great set up. Hallway leading to room smelled really gross. Smell was there all 3 days we stayed. </p><span data-reactid="1885">Carlos</span><span data-reactid="1886">2014-10-21T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1887"><p data-reactid="1888">This apt is perfect for a little vacation in the arts district. Walking distance to the beach, the pike outlets, and the markets and shops in the neighborhood were a good vibe for the artsy/live/and young person. Would have loved to have had Netflix or Hulu available. Had a great shared balcony for guests and washer/dryer. Has all the necessities you would need. </p><span data-reactid="1889">April</span><span data-reactid="1890">2017-01-02T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1891"><p data-reactid="1892">Suzi was a kind, gracious and flexible host. The apartment was a great, efficient/ no frills space. There is a neat little indoor/ outdoor common area where the laundry facilities are located, which was really nice. The neighborhood is amazing! Word of caution to peeps traveling with kids. The space is listed as family friendly, but unless you are the parent to children who's volume level never exceeds a 4 and activity level never rises above book reading, this might not be the best place. There is quite literally no room to play in or immediately around the building, so just be mindful of that when booking with kids. On the flip side, this property is in easy walking distance of the beach, beautiful parks, the aquarium, Seaside Village, a gazillion eateries, eclectic shops and a grocery store just around the corner. This was my first airbnb experience and I am very pleased with it. I would definitely stay here again, just maybe with the Hub and not the small ones.</p><span data-reactid="1893">Stephenie</span><span data-reactid="1894">2014-05-27T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                        <div data-reactid="2159">
                         The Turret Room is in the Turret House located in the historic Willmore District of downtown Long Beach. Built in 1906, this Victorian is on the historical building register. The room is private with private bath across the hall. It is a small cozy room best for solo travelers. The property includes a lovely courtyard with outside seating for guests to enjoy. The house is within walking distance of the Convention Center, beaches and lots of downtown action. Public transport is available nearby.
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="2161">
                         The Willmore District of Long Beach is the oldest neighborhood in the city. It is a lovely mix of people from all over the world. The district has recently been and continues to be in transition. Young folks moving in ... older folks staying on. I love the diversity!
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2162">
                         <li data-reactid="2163"><p data-reactid="2164">I had come to Long Beach for business and stayed in the turret room, and was very pleased. The room itself was perfect for me. It's small, but the bed was very comfortable, with a trompe l'oeil on the ceiling. I will definitely stay there again if my work takes me to Long Beach. The room is the size of a closet. I'm 5'3 and my feet were hanging off the bed a little during the night. There was hair in the bed when I pulled the sheets back. The sheets themselves were smelly, so much so that I found it difficult to fall asleep. The shower is ridiculously tiny and a bit dingy. The bedroom itself is claustrophobic. The pictures made it look bigger. There were no toiletries at all. Bummer. I paid for two nights and could only stand one there. So, I went and paid for a hotel room instead, paying twice for one nights accommodations was better than returning here.
